genomic DNA from peripheral white blood cells [10003885067_R01C01]	GSM3173076	Public on Jun 05 2018	Jun 04 2018	Jun 05 2018	genomic	1	peripheral white blood cells	Homo sapiens	Sex: Male	age: 64	study: PREDIMED	array: 450K	waist circumference (cm): 100		genomic DNA	Genomic DNA was extracted and purified from samples using MasterPure™DNA Purification Kit for Blood according to standard instructions	Cy5 and Cy3	Standard Illumina Protocol	9606	"Bisulphite converted DNA from 474 samples from different cohorts were hybridised to the Illumina Infinium 450k Human Methylation Beadchip (DiOGenes-UNAV, EPALIP, Food4Me-UNAV, GEDYMET, ICTUS, NUGENOB-UNAV, PREDIMED-UNAV, RESMENA, NormoP) or Infinium MethylationEPIC Beadchip (OBEKIT)."	Arrays were imaged using Illumina hiScanSQ platform	10003885067_R01C01	"After obtaining intensity data from minfi R package, filtering probes is performed in probes with a detection p-value above 0.01 in one or more samples, probes with a beadcount <3 in at least 5% of samples,probes non-cpg, probes with SNPs as identified in Nordlund et al, probes that align to multiple locations as identified in Nordlund et al and probes on the X or Y by champ.filter function of ChAMP version 1.11.0.  After filtering probes, intra-cell type normalization is done using Subset-quantile Within Array Normalization (SWAN) method.  After SWAN normalization, magnitude of batch effects are assessed and corrected using the ComBat normalization method.  To correct for the differences in methylation resulting from differences in cellular heterogeneity, the Houseman correction was used (Houseman et al. 2012)."	Matrix_processed.txt: Normalized Average Beta using SWAN (Subset-quantile Within Array Normalization) normalization of ChAMP R package	Matrix_signal_intensities.txt: Unmethylated and methylated signal intensities by getMeth and getUnmet function of minfi R package. To correct for the differences in methylation resulting from differences in cellular heterogeneity, the Houseman correction was used (Houseman et al. 2012)." After filtering probes, intra-cell type normalization is done using Subset-quantile Within Array Normalization (SWAN) method.  After SWAN normalization, magnitude of batch effects are assessed and corrected using the ComBat normalization method.  To correct for the differences in methylation resulting from differences in cellular heterogeneity, the Houseman correction was used (Houseman et al. 2012)." To correct for the differences in methylation resulting from differences in cellular heterogeneity, the Houseman correction was used (Houseman et al. 2012)." To correct for the differences in methylation resulting from differences in cellular heterogeneity, the Houseman correction was used (Houseman et al. 2012)." Arrays were imaged using Illumina hiScanSQ platform	200078650054_R02C01	"After obtaining intensity data from minfi R package, filtering probes is performed in probes with a detection p-value above 0.01 in one or more samples, probes with a beadcount <3 in at least 5% of samples,probes non-cpg, probes with SNPs as identified in Nordlund et al, probes that align to multiple locations as identified in Nordlund et al and probes on the X or Y by champ.filter function of ChAMP version 1.11.0.  After filtering probes, intra-cell type normalization is done using Subset-quantile Within Array Normalization (SWAN) method.  After SWAN normalization, magnitude of batch effects are assessed and corrected using the ComBat normalization method.  To correct for the differences in methylation resulting from differences in cellular heterogeneity, the Houseman correction was used (Houseman et al. 2012)." To correct for the differences in methylation resulting from differences in cellular heterogeneity, the Houseman correction was used (Houseman et al. 2012)." After filtering probes, intra-cell type normalization is done using Subset-quantile Within Array Normalization (SWAN) method.  After SWAN normalization, magnitude of batch effects are assessed and corrected using the ComBat normalization method.  To correct for the differences in methylation resulting from differences in cellular heterogeneity, the Houseman correction was used (Houseman et al. 2012)." After filtering probes, intra-cell type normalization is done using Subset-quantile Within Array Normalization (SWAN) method.  After SWAN normalization, magnitude of batch effects are assessed and corrected using the ComBat normalization method.  To correct for the differences in methylation resulting from differences in cellular heterogeneity, the Houseman correction was used (Houseman et al. 2012)." After SWAN normalization, magnitude of batch effects are assessed and corrected using the ComBat normalization method.  To correct for the differences in methylation resulting from differences in cellular heterogeneity, the Houseman correction was used (Houseman et al. 2012)."
